Equations (all):
{ AND(?y, ?x) = AND(?x, ?y)
  EQ(?x, ?y) = EQ(?y, ?x)
  GE(?x, MAX(?y, ?z)) = GE(?x, MAX(?z, ?y))
  GT(?x, MAX(?y, ?z)) = GT(?x, MAX(?z, ?y))
  MIN(?a, ?b) = MIN(?b, ?a)
  MUL(?a, ?b) = MUL(?b, ?a)
  OR(?y, ?x) = OR(?x, ?y)
  PLUS(?a, ?b) = PLUS(?b, ?a)
